<s> it is permitted thee <\s>
<s> draw thou 85 his spirit from its springs as thou find'st power seize him and lead him on thy downward path and stand ashamed when failure teaches thee that a good man even in his darkest longings is well aware of the right way <\s>
<s> mephistopheles well and good <\s>
<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>
<s> ay dust shall he devour and that with pleasure like my old paramour the famous snake <\s>
<s> 95 the lord pray come here when it suits you for i never had much dislike for people of your sort <\s>
<s> and among all the spirits who rebelled the knave was ever the least tedious to me <\s>
<s> the active spirit of man soon sleeps and soon 100 he seeks unbroken quiet therefore i have given him the devil for a companion who may provoke him to some sort of work and must create forever but ye pure children of god enjoy eternal beauty 105 let that which ever operates and lives clasp you within the limits of its love and seize with sweet and melancholy thoughts the floating phantoms of its loveliness <\s>
<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>
<s> civil enough is the same god almighty to talk so freely with the devil himself <\s>
<s> scene 2 may day night <\s>
<s> the hartz mountain a desolate country <\s>
<s> mephistopheles would you not like a broomstick <\s>
<s> as for me i wish i had a good stout ram to ride for we are still far from the appointed place <\s>
<s> faust this knotted staff is help enough for me whilst i feel fresh upon my legs <\s>
<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>
<s> 10 already spring kindles the birchen spray and the hoar pines already feel her breath shall she not work also within our limbs <\s>
<s> mephistopheles nothing of such an influence do i feel <\s>
<s> my body is all wintry and i wish 15 the flowers upon our path were frost and snow <\s>
<s> but see how melancholy rises now dimly uplifting her belated beam the blank unwelcome round of the red moon and gives so bad a light that every step 20 one stumbles gainst some crag <\s>
<s> with your permission i'll call on ignis fatuus to our aid i see one yonder burning jollily <\s>
<s> may i request that you would favour us with your bright company <\s>
<s> 25 why should you blaze away there to no purpose <\s>
<s> pray be so good as light us up this way <\s>
<s> ignis fatuus with reverence be it spoken i will try to overcome the lightness of my nature our course you know is generally zigzag <\s>

<s> your worship thinks you have to deal with men <\s>

<s> 35 only consider that to night this mountain is all enchanted and if jack a lantern shows you his way though you should miss your own you ought not to be too exact with him <\s>
<s> faust mephistopheles and ignis fatuus in alternate chorus the limits of the sphere of dream 40 the bounds of true and false are past <\s>
<s> lead us on thou wandering gleam lead us onward far and fast to the wide the desert waste <\s>
<s> but see how swift advance and shift 45 trees behind trees row by row how clift by clift rocks bend and lift their frowning foreheads as we go <\s>
<s> the giant snouted crags ho <\s>
<s> how they snort and how they blow <\s>
<s> 50 through the mossy sods and stones stream and streamlet hurry down a rushing throng <\s>
<s> a sound of song beneath the vault of heaven is blown <\s>
<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>
<s> 85 tell me shall we go or stay <\s>

<s> trees and masses intercept 90 the sight and wisps on every side are puffed up and multiplied <\s>

<s> 70 brake 1824 lake 1822 <\s>
<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> does not sir mammon gloriously illuminate his palace for this festival it is 115 a pleasure which you had not known before <\s>

<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>
<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>

<s> mephistopheles well and good <\s>
<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>
<s> ay dust shall he devour and that with pleasure like my old paramour the famous snake <\s>
<s> 95 the lord pray come here when it suits you for i never had much dislike for people of your sort <\s>
<s> and among all the spirits who rebelled the knave was ever the least tedious to me <\s>
<s> the active spirit of man soon sleeps and soon 100 he seeks unbroken quiet therefore i have given him the devil for a companion who may provoke him to some sort of work and must create forever but ye pure children of god enjoy eternal beauty 105 let that which ever operates and lives clasp you within the limits of its love and seize with sweet and melancholy thoughts the floating phantoms of its loveliness <\s>
<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>
<s> civil enough is the same god almighty to talk so freely with the devil himself <\s>

<s> the hartz mountain a desolate country <\s>
<s> mephistopheles would you not like a broomstick <\s>

<s> faust this knotted staff is help enough for me whilst i feel fresh upon my legs <\s>
<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>
<s> 10 already spring kindles the birchen spray and the hoar pines already feel her breath shall she not work also within our limbs <\s>
<s> mephistopheles nothing of such an influence do i feel <\s>
<s> my body is all wintry and i wish 15 the flowers upon our path were frost and snow <\s>
<s> but see how melancholy rises now dimly uplifting her belated beam the blank unwelcome round of the red moon and gives so bad a light that every step 20 one stumbles gainst some crag <\s>
<s> with your permission i'll call on ignis fatuus to our aid i see one yonder burning jollily <\s>
<s> may i request that you would favour us with your bright company <\s>

<s> pray be so good as light us up this way <\s>

<s> faust mephistopheles and ignis fatuus in alternate chorus the limits of the sphere of dream 40 the bounds of true and false are past <\s>
<s> lead us on thou wandering gleam lead us onward far and fast to the wide the desert waste <\s>

<s> how they snort and how they blow <\s>
<s> 50 through the mossy sods and stones stream and streamlet hurry down a rushing throng <\s>
<s> a sound of song beneath the vault of heaven is blown <\s>
<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>

<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>

<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>

<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>

<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>

<s> 95 the lord pray come here when it suits you for i never had much dislike for people of your sort <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>
<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>
<s> 10 already spring kindles the birchen spray and the hoar pines already feel her breath shall she not work also within our limbs <\s>
<s> mephistopheles nothing of such an influence do i feel <\s>

<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>

<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>
<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> mephistopheles would you not like a broomstick <\s>
<s> as for me i wish i had a good stout ram to ride for we are still far from the appointed place <\s>
<s> faust this knotted staff is help enough for me whilst i feel fresh upon my legs <\s>
<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>
<s> 10 already spring kindles the birchen spray and the hoar pines already feel her breath shall she not work also within our limbs <\s>
<s> mephistopheles nothing of such an influence do i feel <\s>
<s> my body is all wintry and i wish 15 the flowers upon our path were frost and snow <\s>
<s> but see how melancholy rises now dimly uplifting her belated beam the blank unwelcome round of the red moon and gives so bad a light that every step 20 one stumbles gainst some crag <\s>
<s> with your permission i'll call on ignis fatuus to our aid i see one yonder burning jollily <\s>
<s> may i request that you would favour us with your bright company <\s>
<s> 25 why should you blaze away there to no purpose <\s>
<s> pray be so good as light us up this way <\s>
<s> ignis fatuus with reverence be it spoken i will try to overcome the lightness of my nature our course you know is generally zigzag <\s>
<s> 30 mephistopheles ha ha <\s>
<s> your worship thinks you have to deal with men <\s>
<s> go straight on in the devil's name or i shall puff your flickering life out <\s>
<s> note 33 shall puff 1824 will blow 1822 <\s>
<s> ignis fatuus well i see you are the master of the house i will accommodate myself to you <\s>
<s> 35 only consider that to night this mountain is all enchanted and if jack a lantern shows you his way though you should miss your own you ought not to be too exact with him <\s>
<s> faust mephistopheles and ignis fatuus in alternate chorus the limits of the sphere of dream 40 the bounds of true and false are past <\s>
<s> lead us on thou wandering gleam lead us onward far and fast to the wide the desert waste <\s>
<s> but see how swift advance and shift 45 trees behind trees row by row how clift by clift rocks bend and lift their frowning foreheads as we go <\s>
<s> the giant snouted crags ho <\s>
<s> how they snort and how they blow <\s>
<s> 50 through the mossy sods and stones stream and streamlet hurry down a rushing throng <\s>
<s> a sound of song beneath the vault of heaven is blown <\s>
<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>
<s> 85 tell me shall we go or stay <\s>
<s> everything around is swept forward onward far away <\s>
<s> trees and masses intercept 90 the sight and wisps on every side are puffed up and multiplied <\s>
<s> notes 48 frowning fawning 1822 <\s>
<s> 70 brake 1824 lake 1822 <\s>
<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>
<s> mephistopheles rare in faith <\s>
<s> does not sir mammon gloriously illuminate his palace for this festival it is 115 a pleasure which you had not known before <\s>
<s> i spy the boisterous guests already <\s>
<s> faust how the children of the wind rage in the air <\s>
<s> with what fierce strokes they fall upon my neck <\s>
<s> note 117 how 1824 now 1822 <\s>
<s> mephistopheles cling tightly to the old ribs of the crag <\s>
<s> for if with them thou warrest in their fierce flight towards the wilderness their breath will sweep thee into dust and drag thy body to a grave in the abyss <\s>
<s> a cloud thickens the night <\s>
<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>
<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>
<s> dost thou not hear <\s>
<s> 140 strange accents are ringing aloft afar anear <\s>
<s> the witches are singing <\s>
<s> the torrent of a raging wizard song streams the whole mountain along <\s>
<s> 145 note 132 shattered scattered rossetti <\s>
<s> chorus of witches the stubble is yellow the corn is green now to the brocken the witches go the mighty multitude here may be seen gathering wizard and witch below <\s>

<s> and hey over stone <\s>

<s> it is permitted thee <\s>
<s> draw thou 85 his spirit from its springs as thou find'st power seize him and lead him on thy downward path and stand ashamed when failure teaches thee that a good man even in his darkest longings is well aware of the right way <\s>
<s> mephistopheles well and good <\s>
<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>
<s> ay dust shall he devour and that with pleasure like my old paramour the famous snake <\s>
<s> 95 the lord pray come here when it suits you for i never had much dislike for people of your sort <\s>
<s> and among all the spirits who rebelled the knave was ever the least tedious to me <\s>
<s> the active spirit of man soon sleeps and soon 100 he seeks unbroken quiet therefore i have given him the devil for a companion who may provoke him to some sort of work and must create forever but ye pure children of god enjoy eternal beauty 105 let that which ever operates and lives clasp you within the limits of its love and seize with sweet and melancholy thoughts the floating phantoms of its loveliness <\s>
<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>
<s> civil enough is the same god almighty to talk so freely with the devil himself <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>

<s> 50 through the mossy sods and stones stream and streamlet hurry down a rushing throng <\s>
<s> a sound of song beneath the vault of heaven is blown <\s>
<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> does not sir mammon gloriously illuminate his palace for this festival it is 115 a pleasure which you had not known before <\s>

<s> a cloud thickens the night <\s>
<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>
<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>

<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>
<s> ay dust shall he devour and that with pleasure like my old paramour the famous snake <\s>
<s> 95 the lord pray come here when it suits you for i never had much dislike for people of your sort <\s>
<s> and among all the spirits who rebelled the knave was ever the least tedious to me <\s>
<s> the active spirit of man soon sleeps and soon 100 he seeks unbroken quiet therefore i have given him the devil for a companion who may provoke him to some sort of work and must create forever but ye pure children of god enjoy eternal beauty 105 let that which ever operates and lives clasp you within the limits of its love and seize with sweet and melancholy thoughts the floating phantoms of its loveliness <\s>
<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>
<s> civil enough is the same god almighty to talk so freely with the devil himself <\s>

<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>
<s> 10 already spring kindles the birchen spray and the hoar pines already feel her breath shall she not work also within our limbs <\s>
<s> mephistopheles nothing of such an influence do i feel <\s>
<s> my body is all wintry and i wish 15 the flowers upon our path were frost and snow <\s>
<s> but see how melancholy rises now dimly uplifting her belated beam the blank unwelcome round of the red moon and gives so bad a light that every step 20 one stumbles gainst some crag <\s>

<s> may i request that you would favour us with your bright company <\s>

<s> faust mephistopheles and ignis fatuus in alternate chorus the limits of the sphere of dream 40 the bounds of true and false are past <\s>
<s> lead us on thou wandering gleam lead us onward far and fast to the wide the desert waste <\s>
<s> but see how swift advance and shift 45 trees behind trees row by row how clift by clift rocks bend and lift their frowning foreheads as we go <\s>
<s> the giant snouted crags ho <\s>
<s> how they snort and how they blow <\s>
<s> 50 through the mossy sods and stones stream and streamlet hurry down a rushing throng <\s>
<s> a sound of song beneath the vault of heaven is blown <\s>
<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> how they snort and how they blow <\s>

<s> a sound of song beneath the vault of heaven is blown <\s>
<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> ay dust shall he devour and that with pleasure like my old paramour the famous snake <\s>
<s> 95 the lord pray come here when it suits you for i never had much dislike for people of your sort <\s>
<s> and among all the spirits who rebelled the knave was ever the least tedious to me <\s>
<s> the active spirit of man soon sleeps and soon 100 he seeks unbroken quiet therefore i have given him the devil for a companion who may provoke him to some sort of work and must create forever but ye pure children of god enjoy eternal beauty 105 let that which ever operates and lives clasp you within the limits of its love and seize with sweet and melancholy thoughts the floating phantoms of its loveliness <\s>
<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>
<s> civil enough is the same god almighty to talk so freely with the devil himself <\s>
<s> scene 2 may day night <\s>
<s> the hartz mountain a desolate country <\s>
<s> mephistopheles would you not like a broomstick <\s>
<s> as for me i wish i had a good stout ram to ride for we are still far from the appointed place <\s>
<s> faust this knotted staff is help enough for me whilst i feel fresh upon my legs <\s>
<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>
<s> 10 already spring kindles the birchen spray and the hoar pines already feel her breath shall she not work also within our limbs <\s>
<s> mephistopheles nothing of such an influence do i feel <\s>
<s> my body is all wintry and i wish 15 the flowers upon our path were frost and snow <\s>
<s> but see how melancholy rises now dimly uplifting her belated beam the blank unwelcome round of the red moon and gives so bad a light that every step 20 one stumbles gainst some crag <\s>
<s> with your permission i'll call on ignis fatuus to our aid i see one yonder burning jollily <\s>
<s> may i request that you would favour us with your bright company <\s>
<s> 25 why should you blaze away there to no purpose <\s>
<s> pray be so good as light us up this way <\s>
<s> ignis fatuus with reverence be it spoken i will try to overcome the lightness of my nature our course you know is generally zigzag <\s>

<s> faust mephistopheles and ignis fatuus in alternate chorus the limits of the sphere of dream 40 the bounds of true and false are past <\s>
<s> lead us on thou wandering gleam lead us onward far and fast to the wide the desert waste <\s>
<s> but see how swift advance and shift 45 trees behind trees row by row how clift by clift rocks bend and lift their frowning foreheads as we go <\s>
<s> the giant snouted crags ho <\s>
<s> how they snort and how they blow <\s>
<s> 50 through the mossy sods and stones stream and streamlet hurry down a rushing throng <\s>
<s> a sound of song beneath the vault of heaven is blown <\s>
<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>
<s> 85 tell me shall we go or stay <\s>
<s> everything around is swept forward onward far away <\s>
<s> trees and masses intercept 90 the sight and wisps on every side are puffed up and multiplied <\s>

<s> 70 brake 1824 lake 1822 <\s>
<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> mephistopheles well and good <\s>
<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>
<s> ay dust shall he devour and that with pleasure like my old paramour the famous snake <\s>
<s> 95 the lord pray come here when it suits you for i never had much dislike for people of your sort <\s>
<s> and among all the spirits who rebelled the knave was ever the least tedious to me <\s>
<s> the active spirit of man soon sleeps and soon 100 he seeks unbroken quiet therefore i have given him the devil for a companion who may provoke him to some sort of work and must create forever but ye pure children of god enjoy eternal beauty 105 let that which ever operates and lives clasp you within the limits of its love and seize with sweet and melancholy thoughts the floating phantoms of its loveliness <\s>
<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>
<s> civil enough is the same god almighty to talk so freely with the devil himself <\s>
<s> scene 2 may day night <\s>
<s> the hartz mountain a desolate country <\s>
<s> mephistopheles would you not like a broomstick <\s>
<s> as for me i wish i had a good stout ram to ride for we are still far from the appointed place <\s>
<s> faust this knotted staff is help enough for me whilst i feel fresh upon my legs <\s>
<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>
<s> 10 already spring kindles the birchen spray and the hoar pines already feel her breath shall she not work also within our limbs <\s>
<s> mephistopheles nothing of such an influence do i feel <\s>
<s> my body is all wintry and i wish 15 the flowers upon our path were frost and snow <\s>
<s> but see how melancholy rises now dimly uplifting her belated beam the blank unwelcome round of the red moon and gives so bad a light that every step 20 one stumbles gainst some crag <\s>
<s> with your permission i'll call on ignis fatuus to our aid i see one yonder burning jollily <\s>
<s> may i request that you would favour us with your bright company <\s>
<s> 25 why should you blaze away there to no purpose <\s>
<s> pray be so good as light us up this way <\s>
<s> ignis fatuus with reverence be it spoken i will try to overcome the lightness of my nature our course you know is generally zigzag <\s>

<s> your worship thinks you have to deal with men <\s>

<s> 35 only consider that to night this mountain is all enchanted and if jack a lantern shows you his way though you should miss your own you ought not to be too exact with him <\s>
<s> faust mephistopheles and ignis fatuus in alternate chorus the limits of the sphere of dream 40 the bounds of true and false are past <\s>
<s> lead us on thou wandering gleam lead us onward far and fast to the wide the desert waste <\s>
<s> but see how swift advance and shift 45 trees behind trees row by row how clift by clift rocks bend and lift their frowning foreheads as we go <\s>
<s> the giant snouted crags ho <\s>
<s> how they snort and how they blow <\s>
<s> 50 through the mossy sods and stones stream and streamlet hurry down a rushing throng <\s>
<s> a sound of song beneath the vault of heaven is blown <\s>
<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>
<s> 85 tell me shall we go or stay <\s>

<s> trees and masses intercept 90 the sight and wisps on every side are puffed up and multiplied <\s>

<s> 70 brake 1824 lake 1822 <\s>
<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> does not sir mammon gloriously illuminate his palace for this festival it is 115 a pleasure which you had not known before <\s>

<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>
<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>

<s> mephistopheles well and good <\s>
<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>
<s> ay dust shall he devour and that with pleasure like my old paramour the famous snake <\s>
<s> 95 the lord pray come here when it suits you for i never had much dislike for people of your sort <\s>
<s> and among all the spirits who rebelled the knave was ever the least tedious to me <\s>
<s> the active spirit of man soon sleeps and soon 100 he seeks unbroken quiet therefore i have given him the devil for a companion who may provoke him to some sort of work and must create forever but ye pure children of god enjoy eternal beauty 105 let that which ever operates and lives clasp you within the limits of its love and seize with sweet and melancholy thoughts the floating phantoms of its loveliness <\s>
<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>
<s> civil enough is the same god almighty to talk so freely with the devil himself <\s>

<s> the hartz mountain a desolate country <\s>
<s> mephistopheles would you not like a broomstick <\s>

<s> faust this knotted staff is help enough for me whilst i feel fresh upon my legs <\s>
<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>
<s> 10 already spring kindles the birchen spray and the hoar pines already feel her breath shall she not work also within our limbs <\s>
<s> mephistopheles nothing of such an influence do i feel <\s>
<s> my body is all wintry and i wish 15 the flowers upon our path were frost and snow <\s>
<s> but see how melancholy rises now dimly uplifting her belated beam the blank unwelcome round of the red moon and gives so bad a light that every step 20 one stumbles gainst some crag <\s>
<s> with your permission i'll call on ignis fatuus to our aid i see one yonder burning jollily <\s>
<s> may i request that you would favour us with your bright company <\s>

<s> pray be so good as light us up this way <\s>

<s> faust mephistopheles and ignis fatuus in alternate chorus the limits of the sphere of dream 40 the bounds of true and false are past <\s>
<s> lead us on thou wandering gleam lead us onward far and fast to the wide the desert waste <\s>

<s> how they snort and how they blow <\s>
<s> 50 through the mossy sods and stones stream and streamlet hurry down a rushing throng <\s>
<s> a sound of song beneath the vault of heaven is blown <\s>
<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>

<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>

<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>

<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>

<s> 90 i am not in much doubt about my bet and if i lose then tis your turn to crow enjoy your triumph then with a full breast <\s>

<s> 95 the lord pray come here when it suits you for i never had much dislike for people of your sort <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>
<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>

<s> what good 5 is there in making short a pleasant way <\s>
<s> to creep along the labyrinths of the vales and climb those rocks where ever babbling springs precipitate themselves in waterfalls is the true sport that seasons such a path <\s>
<s> 10 already spring kindles the birchen spray and the hoar pines already feel her breath shall she not work also within our limbs <\s>
<s> mephistopheles nothing of such an influence do i feel <\s>

<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>

<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> sweet notes of love the speaking tones 55 of this bright day sent down to say that paradise on earth is known resound around beneath above <\s>
<s> all we hope and all we love finds a voice in this blithe strain 60 which wakens hill and wood and rill and vibrates far o'er field and vale and which echo like the tale of old times repeats again <\s>
<s> near nearer now 65 the sound of song the rushing throng <\s>
<s> are the screech the lapwing and the jay all awake as if twere day <\s>
<s> see with long legs and belly wide a salamander in the brake <\s>
<s> 70 every root is like a snake and along the loose hillside with strange contortions through the night curls to seize or to affright and animated strong and many 75 they dart forth polypus antennae to blister with their poison spume the wanderer <\s>
<s> through the dazzling gloom the many coloured mice that thread the dewy turf beneath our tread 80 in troops each other's motions cross through the heath and through the moss and in legions intertangled the fire flies flit and swarm and throng till all the mountain depths are spangled <\s>

<s> mephistopheles now vigorously seize my skirt and gain this pinnacle of isolated crag <\s>
<s> one may observe with wonder from this point 95 how mammon glows among the mountains <\s>
<s> faust ay and strangely through the solid depth below a melancholy light like the red dawn shoots from the lowest gorge of the abyss of mountains lightning hitherward there rise 100 pillars of smoke here clouds float gently by here the light burns soft as the enkindled air or the illumined dust of golden flowers and now it glides like tender colours spreading and now bursts forth in fountains from the earth 105 and now it winds one torrent of broad light through the far valley with a hundred veins and now once more within that narrow corner masses itself into intensest splendour <\s>
<s> and near us see sparks spring out of the ground 110 like golden sand scattered upon the darkness the pinnacles of that black wall of mountains that hems us in are kindled <\s>

<s> how the tempest crashes through the forest <\s>
<s> the owls fly out in strange affright the columns of the evergreen palaces are split and shattered the roots creak and stretch and groan 130 and ruinously overthrown the trunks are crushed and shattered by the fierce blast's unconquerable stress <\s>
<s> over each other crack and crash they all in terrible and intertangled fall 135 and through the ruins of the shaken mountain the airs hiss and howl it is not the voice of the fountain nor the wolf in his midnight prowl <\s>

<s> heaven closes the archangels exeunt mephistopheles from time to time i visit the old fellow 110 and i take care to keep on good terms with him <\s>
